## LEGAL FRAMEWORK

### Fraud Upon the Court

Fraud upon the court vitiates all orders flowing from the fraud. *Hazel-Atlas Glass Co. v. Hartford-Empire Co.*, 322 U.S. 238 (1944). A judgment obtained through fraud is void and may be vacated at any time. MCR 2.612(C)(1)(c) authorizes relief from judgment for fraud, misrepresentation, or other misconduct.

### Fruit of the Poisonous Tree

Evidence and orders derived from an initial unconstitutional or fraudulent act must be suppressed. *Wong Sun v. United States*, 371 U.S. 471 (1963). The doctrine applies in civil context when the initial tainted act is a constitutional violation. If the PPO was obtained through perjury, ALL subsequent orders, custody modifications, and restrictions based on that PPO are tainted fruit.

### The Cascade

```
FALSE PPO PETITION (perjury)
  → PPO Granted (tainted)
    → Custody Modification (fruit of tainted PPO)
      → Parenting Time Restrictions (fruit)
        → August 8, 2025 Ex-Parte Order (compounded fruit)
          → ALL current restrictions on Andrew Pigors (illegitimate)
```

## 5. EX-PARTE ORDER VIOLATIONS — MCL 722.27a(3)

The August 8, 2025 order modified custody/parenting time without the notice and hearing required by MCL 722.27a(3).

**Filing Relevance:** F3 (judge violated statutory requirements), F4 (§1983 due process deprivation), F5 (MSC statutory violation)
